<text>The Snug is remeniscent of a speakeasy. Tucked in around the side of the main stretch off R St, you'll walk through a large set of wooden doors into the dim but bustling bar. The Snug is decorated with classic wallpaper, lounge chairs, wall sconces, and a warthog. Despite it being busy, the bartenders are efficient. We had drinks in hand minutes after arriving. The cocktail choices are well crafted and interesting. If a classic cocktail isn't your jam, there is a great selection of local beers on tap and wine as well.

<UserId.>104677630795965555961</UserId.>< Text>
This place is really different for a Sacramento bar. It gives me a feel of unique "snug" places you get in New York. And to top it off, the Penicillin is untouchable here! Hands down 1 of the best Penicillins I've had.

My only complaint (as my fam and I have come here ALOT) was that the service was really bad a certain night at the bar. Pretty disappointed in the racial profiling. Lindsay and Tony- who are known as great bartenders- provided no service as we sat there. Lindsay ignored us and helped other customers that came up to the bar after us. Tony at least acknowledged us but didn't bother to even ask if he could get something started for us, as he clearly wasn't making anyone else's drinks at that moment. Eventually we found seating else where and got serviced by Carrie- who made up for the lack of customer service from them. Those drinks and the quality of them "now" may still keep some customers happy, but you definitely are not respected as person with character. You should be aware of how you treat your customers.</Text>

<rate>5<//rate><text>What a beautiful venue. My now wife and I got married here in October and we cannot say enough good things about Catta Verdera and their staff.

When picking a venue we felt it was important to pick a place that we connected with. We also felt it was important to connect with the people we would be working with. Jim and Christina were fantastic people. We worked mostly with Christina and she was just so amazing throughout the entire process. She explained everything very well, even multiple times if we forgot and was so pleasant the entire time.

The bride and groom suites were outstanding! The bridal suite is ENORMOUS and everything a bride could want for getting ready. They had staff on hand to get drinks and food at both suites. The groom‚Äôs suite is about just what you would expect, a nice room, not overly sized with a bathroom (no shower) and nice furniture with a nice patio and good places nearby to take photos.

They have a beautiful outdoor ceremony area and picturesque landscapes to back it up. We were originally supposed to have an outdoor ceremony and indoor reception. Our plans changed a few hours before the ceremony was supposed to start due to the forecasted rain. The decision to move the ceremony inside was made and it was beautiful. We never imagined the ceremony inside and no one would have ever guessed that it was not supposed to be that way from the beginning. The way they set up the room you almost wouldn't know that it was also the reception area. Their team did a great job getting everything set up for the ceremony and broken down and ready for the reception.

The food was OUTSTANDING. Not even our pickiest guest had anything bad to say. They also worked with us during the planning process to accommodate our guests with food allergies.

We had an amazing wedding day, their staff made the rain a non-factor for us and took care of everything. Most people think when something like that happens it's a disaster but both of us felt like everything went on without the notion of a hiccup. If amazing food and flawless landscape is important to you in finding your perfect venue we would highly recommend Catta Verdera.<//text>< pics>

< review>
Best burgers I have ever had.

The atmosphere is great, its not what you would expect for how good it is though. They have TVs displaying sports or news or whatever else, which doesn't really bother me one way or the other. The owners are the nicest people. They love to come and talk to you like you were a close friend, which is amazing. They are down to earth, and love to hear your honest feedback. They are always thinking up new ideas to make the customers happier.

Their location is a bit strange, and its easy to miss where you pull in. I am a new driver though, and I could do it easily. The location has a very homey feel to it, which I adore.

So! The food. Their menu, which I heard that they are freshening up a bit, looks a little daunting. It isn't. It is in big font, which makes it easy to read, but makes it look kinda like the menu is bigger than it is. What I got this last time was the make your own burger. You get to choose your meat, cheese, toppings, insides of the burger, your side, the works. I got my burger medium rare, and it was delicious. I have leftovers waiting for me in the fridge it filled me up so well! (They've even won awards as far as I know!)

These wonderful people need to see some more love. They are incredible, and so very sweet. We need to get the news out there about them.

I hope my review helped with the decision to eat there!< /review>

< user_name>
Darrien Boling<//user_name>
<review>Boomerang's is a unique burger joint in the Clairemont Mesa area. It's not very noticeable from the main road, and even from the parking lot, the entrance is hidden away in a little courtyard. First, the criticisms: The building seems older and not well taken care of. This is emphasized by the hodgepodge decorations (but not in a good way). There was also no music (though I did notice ceiling speakers), which contributed to making the ambiance awkwardly quiet since there were few guests when we went and the restaurant is surprisingly large. On the positive side, our waiter (Jose) was very friendly and attentive. I had a 1/2lb Bad Breath Burger with Chilli Pepper Onion Rings. I love garlic; so, having garlic mixed into the Patty was amazing. Staying true to it's name, the cheese of choice is gorgonzola, and it is slathers with just enough fresh horseradish. Grilled onions galore top the creation, and on the side comes a creamy garlic-horseradish mayo. The Chilli Pepper Onion Rings have a wonderful crunch and get an added kick by the jalapeno topping. It comes with habanero ketchup which is good, though not as spicy as I hoped for, given the name. Overall, it's a delicious meal in an okay space. But, I think it's worth a shot!<//review><Pictures>None< /Pictures></record>

<time>1483308972460<//time>< text>
We ordered 2 apps and 2 entrees with salads. Approx 68 bucks with 15% tip.
The salads were ok. The rest of the food was awful.
I called the restaurant to see if the chef had a stroke or something, and let them know the food was well below expectations.
The man who answered the phone interrupted me repeatedly and said I was being "mean" when I told him the mac and cheese was a soggy old inedible mess with separated cheese sauce- totally microwaved.
He declared that all was "made to order" and when I suggested he hire a new chef (I have to now assume I was speaking to the sensitive chef?) he tried to blame the yelp eat24 driver on the poor quality food.
I'll post pics of the Philly cheesesteak- lettuce and tomatoes- whyyy?? And a big ole hunk of overdone steak, apparently couldn't be bothered to slice it thin- or at all.
Burger- super soggy bun. When an order is going out for delivery you should know how to package it.
And the worst offender- which made me put down my fork and start this review- the mac and cheese. Disgusting. Mushy, greasy, separated sauce and pasta was cooked to death.
Calamari- frozen strips. I want rings and tentacles, you know- real food.
All of it was flavorless and overdone. Huge portions of low quality product. Oh boy!<//text>

<name>Lady Patriot 711<//name><Review>We love to dine at Tommy Bahamas in the Corona del Mar Plaza. We came in at about 3 p.m. for a late lunch early dinner and we were seated immediately on a Saturday. This restaurant has been completely remodeled with high ceilings, Breezy open doors to the sidewalk and Patio, and a great rectangular bar sitting right in the middle of the restaurant. Aside from the relaxing beachy elegant atmosphere the food is always divine. I had the crab and avocado salad and my husband had the filet mignon salad but that was not the the only star in the show. We ordered the grilled scallop sliders to start with and honestly I've never tasted a more tender juicy fresh from the ocean scallop in my life.
